<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>4.3 PRO FORMA 
SUMMARY CONSOLIDATED STATEMENT OF FINANCIAL PERFORMANCE</U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The pro forma 
consolidated summary statement of financial performance of Magellan set out 
below has
been prepared to illustrate the financial performance of Magellan following 
completion of the Offer
assuming that:
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Magellan completes the acquisition of all MPAL Shares currently on issue
which Magellan does not own; and</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the transaction had taken place as of 30 June&nbsp;2005 (with income 
statement matters deemed to have affected the year to that date).</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The pro forma 
consolidated summary statement of financial performance is intended to be
illustrative only and will not reflect the actual performance as at the date of 
this Bidder&#146;s
Statement or at the conclusion of the Offer.
</DIV>

<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 12pt; margin-top: 12pt">5. ABOUT MPAL
</DIV>
<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>5.1</U> 
<U>DISCLAIMER</U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The following 
description of MPAL and the financial information concerning MPAL contained in 
this
section have been prepared by Magellan using publicly available information and 
certain information
provided to Magellan by Magellan&#146;s nominees on the board of MPAL. 
Information in this document
concerning MPAL&#146;s business has not been independently verified and Magellan
has not conducted any
due diligence on MPAL&#146;s business. To the extent permitted by law, Magellan 
does not make any
representation or warranty, express or implied, as to the currency, accuracy or 
completeness of
such information.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The primary sources 
of information about MPAL&#146;s business used by Magellan are as follows:
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>MPAL&#146;s 2005 Annual Report; and</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>MPAL&#146;s website.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Further information 
about MPAL (including copies of financial statements) can be found on 
MPAL&#146;s
website: www.magpet.com.au.
</DIV>
<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>5.2</U> 
<U>OVERVIEW OF MPAL AND ITS PRINCIPAL BUSINESS ACTIVITIES </U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">MPAL is engaged in 
the sale of oil and gas in the exploration for and development of oil and gas
reserves.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">MPAL&#146;s major 
assets are two petroleum production leases covering the Mereenie Oil and Gas 
Field
<B>(Mereenie) </B>(35% working interest) and one petroleum production lease 
covering the Palm Valley Gas
Field <B>(Palm Valley) </B>(52% working interest). Both fields are located in 
the Amadeus Basin in the
Northern Territory.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Mereenie Oil and
Gas Field</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">MPAL has a 35% 
interest and Santos Limited, the operator, has a 65% interest in Mereenie. 
MPAL&#146;s
share of the remaining Mereenie proved developed oil reserves (net of 
royalties), based upon
contract amounts, was approximately 262,000 barrels and 14.6&nbsp;billion cubic 
feet of gas as at 30
June&nbsp;2005. During the 2005 financial year, MPAL&#146;s share of oil sales 
was 136,000 barrels, and its
share of gas sales was 4.3&nbsp;billion cubic feet. Two gas development wells 
were drilled in late 2004
to increase deliverability in order to meet the gas contractual requirements 
until June&nbsp;2009.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Palm Valley Gas 
Field</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">MPAL has a 52.023% 
interest in and is the operator of Palm Valley. Santos Limited owns the
remaining interest in Palm Valley which provides gas to meet the Alice Springs 
and Darwin supply
contracts with the Northern Territory Power and Water Corporation (<B>PAWC</B>) 
and Gasgo Pty Limited
(<B>Gasgo</B>), a wholly owned subsidiary of PAWC.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">MPAL&#146;s share of 
the remaining Palm Valley proved developed reserves, net of royalties, was 10.7
billion cubic feet as at 30 June&nbsp;2005. During fiscal 2005, MPAL&#146;s 
share of gas sales was 2.4
billion cubic feet.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">MPAL drilled an 
additional development well, Palm Valley&#150;11, in 2004. The well was a dry 
hole.
Gasgo paid the cost of the well under the gas supply agreement. The producers 
and Gasgo have agreed
to install additional compression equipment in the field that will assist field 
deliverability
during the remaining Darwin gas contract period. Gasgo will pay for the cost of 
the additional
compression under the gas supply agreement, which is scheduled to be 
commissioned in the field at
the end of 2005. The production lease covering the Palm Valley Field expires in 
November&nbsp;2024.
</DIV>
<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">-32-
</DIV>
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Nockatunga Oil 
Fields</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">MPAL acquired a 
40.936% working interest in the Nockatunga Oil Fields in July&nbsp;2004. Santos 
Limited
is the operator of the fields and holds the remaining interest. The assets 
comprise eight producing
oil fields in Petroleum Leases 33, 50 and 51 together with exploration acreage 
in ATP 267P. The
fields are currently producing approximately 258 barrels of oil per day. During 
fiscal 2005, MPAL&#146;s
share of oil sales was 35,000 barrels. MPAL&#146;s share of the Nockatunga 
Fields&#146; proved developed oil
reserves was approximately 253,000 barrels as at 30 June&nbsp;2005. Petroleum 
Lease 33 expires in April
2007 and Petroleum Leases 50 and 51 expire in June&nbsp;2011.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">A 92 square mile 3D 
seismic survey was undertaken in late 2004 over Petroleum Lease 51 and parts of
PL 33 and ATP 267P. The drilling of three wells, development as well as 
exploration, is planned for
late 2005 at locations identified by the seismic data.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Dingo Gas 
Field</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">MPAL has a 34.3% 
interest in the Dingo Gas Field which is held under a retention licence. No 
market
has emerged for the gas volumes that have been discovered in the Dingo Gas 
Field. The licence
expires in October&nbsp;2008.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Maryborough 
Basin</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">MPAL holds a 100% 
interest in exploration permit ATP 613P and has applications pending for permits
ATP 674P and ATP 733P in the Maryborough Basin in Queensland.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Cooper/Eromanga 
Basin</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>PEL 94 and PEL 
95</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">During fiscal 1999,
MPAL (50%) and Beach Petroleum Limited were successful in binding for two
exploration blocks (PEL94 and PEL95) in South Australia&#146;s Cooper Basin. 
Aldinga-1 was completed in
September&nbsp;2002 and began producing in May&nbsp;2003 at 80 barrels of oil 
per day. By June&nbsp;2005,
production had declined to about 25 barrels of oil per day. Petroleum Production
Licence 210 was
granted over the Aldinga field in December&nbsp;2004. During July&nbsp;2004, the
Waitpinga-1 well was drilled
in PEL95 and the Almonta-1 well was drilled in PEL95 during April&nbsp;2005. 
Both wells were dry holes.
Black Rock Petroleum NL contributed to the cost of drilling the Myponga-1 well 
in June&nbsp;2004 to earn
a 15% interest in the PEL94 permit. MPAL&#146;s interest in PEL94 was reduced to
35%. Black Rock
Petroleum NL subsequently assigned its interest in PEL94 to Victoria Petroleum 
NL.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>PEL 110 and PELA 
116</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">During fiscal year 
2001, MPAL and Beach Petroleum Limited were successful in bidding for two
additional exploration blocks, PEL 110 (37.5%) and PELA 116 (50%) in the Cooper 
Basin. PEL 110 was
granted in February&nbsp;2003. The application for PELA 116 has been withdrawn. 
During July&nbsp;2005, the
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Yanerbie-1 well was 
drilled in PEL 110. Cooper Energy NL contributed to the cost of the well to
earn a 25% interest in PEL 110 and Enterprise Energy NL contributed to the cost 
of the well to earn
12.5% in any discovery. The well was a dry hole. MPAL has granted Enterprise 
Energy NL the option
to earn 6.25% interest in PEL 110 by funding further exploration in the area. At
30 June&nbsp;2005,
MPAL&#146;s share of the work obligations of the PEL 110 permit totalled 
$0.601&nbsp;million, of which $0.143
was committed.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Kiana-1 
Discovery</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">MPAL farmed into the 
Kiana-1 and Tyringa-1 wells in Great Artesian Oil and Gas&#146; permit PEL 107.
Kiana-1 flowed 1,100 barrels of oil per day and 2.8&nbsp;million cubic feet per 
day on test. Kiana-1 is
currently on production test. MPAL has earned a 30% interest in this discovery.
</DIV>
<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">-33-
</DIV>
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>New Zealand</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>PEP 38222, PEP 
38225 and PEP 38765</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">During fiscal 2002, 
MPAL was granted exploration permit PEP 38222, offshore south of the South
Island of New Zealand. Following a program of seismic processing and 
interpretation, the permit was
surrendered during May&nbsp;2005. In November&nbsp;2003, MPAL was granted permit
PEP 38225, adjacent to PEP
38222. On 30 June&nbsp;2005, MPAL&#146;s contingent work obligations on PEP 
38225 totalled $12.725&nbsp;million.
MPAL has the discretion whether or not to proceed with expenditure of these 
monies MPAL was granted
exploration permit PEP 38765 (12.5%) during February&nbsp;2004. The Miromiro-1 
well was drilled in the
permit during December&nbsp;2004. The well was a dry hole. At 30 June&nbsp;2005,
MPAL&#146;s share of work
obligations on this permit totalled $0.21&nbsp;million, of which none was 
committed.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>United Kingdom</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>PEDL 098 and PEDL 
099</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">During fiscal year 
2001, MPAL acquired an interest in two licences in southern England in the
Weald-Wessex Basin. The licences, PEDL 098 (22.5% interest) in the Isle of Wight
and PEDL 099 (40%
interest) in the Portsdown area of Hampshire, were each granted for a period of 
six years. The
Sandhills-2 well spudded in PEDL 098 during August&nbsp;2005. The UK companies, 
Northern Petroleum and
Montrose Industries funded part of MPAL&#146;s share in the cost of the 
Sandhills-2 well.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>PEDL 112 and PEDL
113</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">During fiscal year 
2002, MPAL acquired two additional licences in southern England. The licences,
PEDL 113 (22.5% interest) in the Isle of Wight and PEDL 112 (33.3% interest) in 
the Kent area on
the margin of the Weald-Wessex Basin were each granted for a period of six 
years.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>PEDL 125 and PEDL
126</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Effective 1 
July&nbsp;2003, MPAL acquired two licences each granted for a period of six 
years in
southern England &#150; PEDL 125 (40% interest) in Hampshire and PEDL 126 (40% 
interest) in West Sussex.
The drilling plans for the Hedge End-2 well in PEDL 125 and Horndean Extension-1
well in PEDL 126
are in progress and spudding of these wells is expected in 2006. The UK company,
Oil Quest
Resources Plc will fund part of MPAL&#146;s share of the cost of the two wells 
to acquire a 10% interest
in each of them.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>PEDL 135, PEDL 
136 and PEDL 137</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Effective 1 
October&nbsp;2004, MPAL was granted a 100% interest in these licences in 
southern England
for six years, each with a drill or drop obligation at the end of the third year
of the term. MPAL
has undertaken a program of seismic data purchase and interpretation.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>PEDL 151, PEDL 
152, PEDL 153, PEDL 154 and PEDL 155</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Effective 1 
October&nbsp;2004, MPAL acquired an additional five licences each granted for a 
period of
six years in southern England being an interest of 11.25%, 22.5%, 33.3%, 50% and
40% in the above
licences respectively. Each licence has a drill or drop obligation at the end of
the third year of
the term. Oil Quest Plc will fund part of MPAL&#146;s share of the PEDL 155 
exploration costs to acquire
10% interest in the licence.
</DIV>

<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt"><TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" 
cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left"><I>3.</I></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><I>EBITDAX represents earnings before depreciation amortisation write-
off of exploration costs,
interest (income), and tax (benefit).</I></TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>

<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>5.4</U> 
<U>FINANCIAL SUMMARY </U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">In summary, 
MPAL&#146;s financial report for the financial year ended 30 June&nbsp;2005 
shows the following:
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>MPAL&#146;s consolidated profit from ordinary activities before write 
off of capitalised
exploration expenditure and income tax was A$8.998&nbsp;million representing an 
increase of 113%
from the previous period. The principal contributing factor was a 16% increases 
in sales
revenue of A$4.106&nbsp;million primarily due to higher oil prices;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>After writing off capitalised exploration expenditure totalling 
A$7.581&nbsp;million and taking
into account an income tax benefit of A$0.117&nbsp;million, profit from ordinary
activities after
income tax was A$1.534&nbsp;million down 52% from the comparable figure in 2004 
of A$3.182&nbsp;million;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Total sales revenue was up 16% (A$4.106&nbsp;million) comprised of an 
increase of 47% in oil sales
revenue principally from the Mereenie and Nocktunga fields and an increase of 3%
in gas sales
revenue;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(d)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Compared on a year-on-year basis, the Statement of Financial Position 
shows a 1% decrease in
shareholders&#146; funds of A$0.801&nbsp;million to A$59.115&nbsp;million and 
the current asset ratio has
increased from 4.2 to 6.3 due to a combination of higher receivables and lower 
payables. Net
cash flows from operating activities has fallen slightly from 
A$16.047&nbsp;million to A$15.984
million; and</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(e)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD>MPAL has cash reserves of approximately A$29&nbsp;million.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>

require MPAL to:

<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>6.1</U> 
<U>GENERAL</U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">This Section&nbsp;6 
sets out Magellan&#146;s intentions with respect to MPAL&#146;s business and

are based on its review and current assessment of MPAL&#146;s business, 
operations and prospects.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Except for changes
and intentions specifically set out in this Section&nbsp;6, Magellan intends, 
based
on the information presently known to it:
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>to continue the business of MPAL;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>not to make any major changes to the business of MPAL or the deployment 
of fixed assets of
MPAL; and</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>

</TR>

</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan&#146;s 
intentions are based on the information known and the circumstances that exist 
at the
date of this Bidder&#146;s Statement.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Final decisions in 
relation to Magellan&#146;s intentions will only be reached in light of all 
material
facts and circumstances. Accordingly, the statements set out in this Section are
statements of
current intention only which may change as new information becomes available or 
circumstances
change.
</DIV>
<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>6.2</U> 
<U>RATIONALE FOR THE OFFER</U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan has made the
Offer as it believes that the current shareholding structure of MPAL has not
provided optimal benefits and transparency as to pricing or market understanding
of MPAL&#146;s assets
nor fostered liquidity or access to capital in either market.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Among the reasons to 
accept Magellan&#146;s Offer are simplification of Magellan&#146;s corporate 
structure,
greater liquidity for investors, access to capital for future strategic 
initiatives or exploration
activities on potentially more favourable terms, opportunities for 
organisational efficiencies and
greater ability to align the strategies of the companies.
</DIV>
<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>6.3</U> 
<U>MAGELLAN&#146;S INTENTIONS UPON ACQUISITION OF 90% OR MORE OF MPAL SHARES</U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">This Section sets out
Magellan&#146;s intentions if it acquires 90% or more of MPAL Shares, if the 
Offer
is declared free of all Conditions and Magellan becomes entitled to proceed to 
compulsory
acquisition under the Corporations Act for the MPAL Shares:
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Compulsory acquisition</B>: Magellan intends to proceed to compulsory
acquisition of the
remaining MPAL Shares in accordance with the provisions of the Corporations 
Act.</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Removal from Official List</B>: Magellan intends to request ASX to 
remove MPAL from the Official
List of the ASX following completion of the Offer.</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Business</B>: Magellan expects MPAL to continue as an oil and gas 
exploration and production
company in substantially the same manner as it is presently operated.</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(d)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Board of Directors and executive management</B>: Magellan will 
maintain the current board of
directors subject to the existing directors&#146; consent. Magellan will also 
seek to retain key
members of the MPAL&#146;s executive management team, whose performance will 
continue to be
reviewed in line with current procedures. Additional members of the executive 
management team
will be added, as appropriate.</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(e)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Employees and consultants</B>: Magellan intends to continue the 
monitoring and review process
which is currently in place in regard to MPAL&#146;s employees and the usage of 
consultancy
services.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">-40-
</DIV>

<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt"><TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0"

position, Magellan intends to review all of MPAL&#146;s important business

including corporate governance, exploration and development efforts, capital 
expenditures,
existing and planned joint ventures, acquisition prospects, and investment 
policies, with the
aim to maximise all shareholder returns.</TD>

the new ownership structure, in</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>co-operation with the MPAL Board, its executive management and taking 
into account the
strategic review undertaken by MPAL&#146;s business development committee.</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>

    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(k)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Cash resources</B>: Magellan believes that MPAL&#146;s existing cash 
resources are currently
sufficient to continue its business without a major effort to raise additional 
capital.</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(l)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Other actions</B>: Magellan intends to undertake all other actions 
consistent with Magellan&#146;s
role and interests of the combined companies and the shareholders.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">If, in the future, 
MPAL does not perform to an acceptable level, Magellan will take whatever action
it deems necessary to maximise its shareholders&#146; returns.
</DIV>
<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>6.4</U> 
<U>MAGELLAN&#146;S INTENTIONS UPON ACQUISITION OF LESS THAN 90% OF MPAL 
SHARES</U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">If Magellan becomes 
entitled to less than 90% of MPAL Shares, Magellan presently intends to allow
the Offer to lapse.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">This Section sets out
Magellan&#146;s intentions if, notwithstanding its present intention, it
subsequently determines to declare the Offer free from the 90% minimum 
acceptance Condition without
becoming entitled to compulsorily acquire the outstanding MPAL Shares.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan reserves its
right to declare the Offer free from the 90% minimum acceptance Condition (or
any other Condition), although it has no present intention to do so. In the 
event that the Offer is
declared free of all Conditions and Magellan achieves a Relevant Interest in 
MPAL of less than 90%
Magellan&#146;s current intentions are as set out below.
</DIV>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 12pt; margin-top: 12pt">7. OFFER 
CONSIDERATION AND IMPLICATIONS FOR ACCEPTING MPAL SHAREHOLDERS
</DIV>
<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>7.1 
CONSIDERATION UNDER THE OFFER</U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The consideration for
the acquisition of the MPAL Shares to which the Offer relates will be
satisfied by the issue of Magellan Shares. In the case of the Offer made under 
this Bidder&#146;s
Statement, MPAL Shareholders may choose to receive Magellan Shares or Magellan 
Shares in the form
of Magellan CDIs.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">MPAL Shareholders who
do not express a choice are deemed to have chosen to receive Magellan Shares
in the form of Magellan CDIs.
</DIV>
<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>7.2 SHARES 
CONSIDERATION</U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Based on the number 
of MPAL Shares on issue as at the date of this Bidder&#146;s Statement, the 
maximum
number of Magellan Shares (to be issued in the form of Magellan CDIs) that would
be required to
settle acceptances under the Offer is 14,667,042 (disregarding rounding for 
fractional
entitlements).
</DIV>
<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>7.3 MAGELLAN 
SHAREHOLDER APPROVAL REQUIRED</U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">NASDAQ Marketplace 
Rule 4350(i) provides that Magellan must obtain shareholder approval if it
wishes to issue Magellan Shares or other securities convertible into Magellan 
Shares if the voting
powers attached to those securities would represent more than 20% of the voting 
power represented
by Magellan&#146;s then existing outstanding securities.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan plans to 
convene a meeting of its shareholders to be held at Hartford, Connecticut to
obtain this shareholder approval. This meeting is expected to be held in January
or February&nbsp;2006.
</DIV>
<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>7.4 MAGELLAN 
CDIS</U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Under the Offer, MPAL
Shareholders are being offered 7 Magellan Shares for every 10 MPAL Shares.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Accepting MPAL 
Shareholders may choose to receive Magellan Shares in the form of Magellan CDIs.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The ASX uses an 
electronic system, called the Clearing House Electronic Subregister System 
(<B>CHESS</B>),
for the clearance and settlement of transactions in securities traded on the 
stock market of the
ASX. Securities of companies incorporated outside of Australia whose governing 
legislation does not
allow the direct use of CHESS, such as Magellan, are traded on ASX as 
&#145;CDIs&#146;. CDIs represent
beneficial interests in the foreign securities and enable Magellan Shares to be 
transferred and
settled electronically using CHESS. The Offer is an offer of Magellan Shares but
Magellan will not
issue Magellan Share certificates to accepting MPAL Shareholders who choose to 
receive Magellan
CDIs. Rather, Magellan will issue holding statements for CDIs. By accepting the 
Offer, such an
accepting MPAL Shareholder will be applying for Magellan Shares to be issued to,
and held by, CDN.
The underlying Magellan Shares are quoted and traded on the stock market of the 
ASX; however, the
CDIs are used to effect the broker to broker settlement of trading in the 
Magellan Shares. Thus,
the beneficial interest in the Magellan Shares is freely transferable 
electronically in CHESS,
subject to applicable law.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The principal 
difference between holding Magellan CDIs and holding the underlying Magellan 
Shares
is that the holder of Magellan CDIs will hold a beneficial interest in the 
equivalent number of
Magellan Shares, but not legal title. The legal title to the underlying Magellan
Shares is instead
held by CDN, which is a wholly owned subsidiary of ASTC, which is in turn a 
wholly owned subsidiary
of the ASX. Thus, using Magellan CDIs, a seller transfers beneficial interest in
the Magellan
Shares to the buyer instead of legal title. See Section&nbsp;7.5 for a summary 
of the rights attaching
to the Magellan CDIs.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Number of CDIs 
issued in relation to Magellan Shares</B>
</DIV>
<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">-43-
</DIV>
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan CDIs are 
structured so that 1 CDI represents 1 Magellan Share. Holders of Magellan CDIs
will be entitled to all the economic benefits of the Magellan Shares, such as 
dividends (if any) as
though they were holders of the legal title.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Magellan 
registers</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan will operate
three registers:
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>a certificated register of Magellan Shares;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>an uncertificated issuer-sponsored subregister of Magellan CDIs; 
and</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>an uncertificated CHESS subregister of Magellan CDIs.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The certificated 
register will be the register of legal title. CDN will be entered on the
certificated register, along with any existing Magellan Shareholders who were 
Magellan&#146;s
shareholders of record prior to the Offer who choose to have their holdings 
remain in certificated
form. The two uncertificated Magellan CDI subregisters combined comprise the 
register of beneficial
interests.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Accepting MPAL 
Shareholders who choose to receive Magellan CDIs may receive Magellan CDIs on 
either
the issuer-sponsored subregister or CHESS subregister. Holding and trading 
Magellan CDIs on the
CHESS subregister has a reduced settlement risk because CHESS settlement results
in the irrevocable
transfer of Magellan CDIs and cash. For accepting MPAL Shareholders who elect to
hold their
Magellan CDIs on the CHESS subregister, Magellan will issue an allotment advice 
that sets out the
number of Magellan CDIs allotted and at the end of the month of allotment, ASTC
(acting on behalf
of Magellan) will provide a Magellan CDI holding statement (similar to a bank 
account statement),
which confirms the number of Magellan CDIs held on the CHESS subregister. If an 
accepting MPAL
Shareholder elects to hold Magellan CDIs on the issuer-sponsored subregister 
rather than the CHESS
subregister, Magellan will issue a Magellan CDI holding statement which sets out
the number of
Magellan CDIs held on the issuer-sponsored subregister. Following distribution 
of these initial
holding statements to all Magellan CDI holders, a holding statement will only be
provided to a
holder at the end of any subsequent month in which the holder buys, sells or 
otherwise transfers
Magellan CDIs. Holders may also request statements at any other time (although 
Magellan or ASTC may
charge a fee for such statements).
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Converting 
Magellan CDIs to Magellan Shares</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">After the successful 
closing of the Offer, holders who do not wish to have their trades settled in
Magellan CDIs may request share certificates representing the Magellan Shares 
by:
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>in the case of issuer-sponsored Magellan CDIs, notifying Magellan&#146;s
Registrar:</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Computershare Investor Services Pty Limited</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left"><B>&nbsp;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>on 1300 55 61 61 (if calling from within Australia) or &#043;61 8 8236 
2300 (if calling from
outside Australia); or</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>in the case of CHESS-sponsored Magellan CDIs, notifying the CHESS 
sponsoring participant (in
most cases, your stockbroker).</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan has been 
informed that the process of surrendering Magellan CDIs for the underlying
Magellan Shares may be completed within 24-48 hours at no cost to the holder.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">ASX does not provide 
any settlement system for certificated Magellan Shares. Settlement of trades
in Magellan Shares that are held in certificated form must be organised between 
the buying and
selling broker for the transaction, which may lead to delay and expense. Thus, 
Magellan believes
that the majority of accepting MPAL Shareholders will prefer to register and 
trade Magellan CDIs on
the CHESS subregister.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Converting 
Magellan Shares to Magellan CDIs</B>
</DIV>
<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">-44-
</DIV>
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Holders of Magellan 
Shares may also transfer their Magellan Shares to CDN and receive Magellan CDIs
(in the same manner as above) which may then be traded on ASX. The likelihood of
holders of
Magellan Shares converting them to Magellan CDIs and vice versa will depend on a
number of factors
including the price at which Magellan Shares and Magellan CDIs trade on NASDAQ 
and ASX, brokerage
rates and prevailing exchange rates.
</DIV>
<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>7.5</U>
<U>RIGHTS ATTACHING TO MAGELLAN CDIS UNDER THE ASTC SETTLEMENT RULES</U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The relationship 
between Magellan, CDN and holders of Magellan CDIs is governed in part by the 
ASTC
Settlement Rules which have the force of law under the Corporations Act. The 
following is a summary
of the rights and obligations of these parties as set out in the ASTC Settlement
Rules:
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Title</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan must cause 
the legal title to the underlying Magellan Shares in respect of the Magellan
CDIs to be vested in CDN. The beneficial title to the underlying Magellan Shares
is vested in the
holders of Magellan CDIs. The holders of Magellan CDIs are to receive all direct
economic benefits
and any other entitlements with respect to the Magellan Shares. CDN is not to 
dispose of any of the
Magellan Shares unless authorised by the ASTC Settlement Rules, and is not able 
to create any
interest that is inconsistent with the title of the holders of Magellan CDIs.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Registers</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan must ensure 
that at all times the total number of Magellan CDIs on the issuer sponsored
subregister of Magellan CDIs and the uncertificated CHESS subregister of 
Magellan CDIs reconciles
with the number of Magellan Shares registered in the name of CDN on the Magellan
Share register.
Magellan must make available for inspection the Magellan Share register and the 
Magellan CDI
register as if that register were a register of securities of an Australian 
listed public company.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Transfer</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Unless permitted by 
the Listing Rules, Magellan or CDN must not refuse nor fail to register, nor
give effect to, nor otherwise interfere with the processing and registration of 
a transfer of
Magellan CDIs. Any obligation to transfer a quantity of Magellan Shares shall be
made by initiating
a transfer of the corresponding quantity of Magellan CDIs in respect of the 
Magellan Shares.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Dividends</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Any dividend declared
in respect of the Magellan Shares vested in CDN is to be distributed to the
holders of the Magellan CDIs. CDN is taken to have directed Magellan to 
distribute any dividend
that would otherwise be payable to it under Magellan&#146;s restated certificate
of incorporation to the
holders of Magellan CDIs.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan has never 
declared or paid dividends on Magellan Shares and has no current intention to
change this policy. See Section&nbsp;3.10 for details.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Bonus issues, 
rights issues and reconstructions</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan must 
administer all bonus issues, rights issues, reconstructions and mergers that 
result
in the issue of additional or replacement Magellan Shares so that the benefits 
are distributed to
holders of Magellan CDIs on the same terms as would otherwise have applied if 
the holders of
Magellan CDIs were the holders of the Magellan Shares.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Voting</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">CDN as a shareholder 
of record of Magellan will receive notice of all Magellan shareholder meetings
and be entitled to attend and vote at Magellan shareholder meetings.
</DIV>
<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">-45-
</DIV>
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Holders of Magellan 
CDIs are not entitled as of right to attend meetings of holders of Magellan
Shares; however, Magellan will invite holders of Magellan CDIs to attend 
Magellan shareholder
meetings; but they will not be permitted to vote other than by direction to CDN.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan must send a 
notice of the shareholder meeting to each holder of Magellan CDIs at the
address recorded in the Magellan CDI register if any meeting is convened for the
holders of
Magellan Shares. The notice must:
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>inform the holder of Magellan CDIs of their rights to direct CDN on how 
it should vote with
respect to the resolutions described in the notice;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>make provision for a direction to be given by the holders of Magellan 
CDIs in relation to how
CDN should so vote;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>make appropriate arrangements to collect and process any direction by 
holders of Magellan
CDIs and provide CDN with a report in writing that clearly shows how CDN must 
exercise its
right to vote by proxy at the Magellan shareholder meeting, in sufficient time 
to enable CDN
to lodge a proxy for the meeting.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Following the time 
and day by which holders of Magellan CDIs must provide their direction to CDN,
CDN will calculate the number of votes in favour of the resolution, the number 
of votes against the
resolution and the number of votes abstaining. CDN will then appoint 2 proxies. 
One of the 2
proxies will indicate the number of Magellan CDIs in favour of the resolution 
described in the
proxy, and the second proxy will indicate the number of Magellan CDIs against 
the resolution
described in the proxy.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">If it is necessary or
appropriate that a meeting of the holders of Magellan CDIs be convened, the
notice and conduct of the meeting will be held in accordance with the provisions
of Magellan&#146;s
Restated Certificate of Incorporation, as amended (<B>Magellan Restated 
Certificate of Incorporation</B>)
and amended and restated By-Laws as of 22 July&nbsp;2004 (<B>Magellan By-
Laws</B>).
</DIV>
<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>7.6</U> 
<U>RIGHTS ATTACHING TO MAGELLAN SHARES</U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The following 
information is a summary of the Magellan Restated Certificate of Incorporation 
and
Magellan By-Laws. MPAL Shareholders have the right to obtain a copy of the 
Magellan Restated
Certificate of Incorporation and By-Laws, free of charge, from Magellan during 
the Offer Period.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Each Magellan Share 
confers on its holder:
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The right to vote at a general meeting of
shareholders (whether present in person or by any
representative, proxy or attorney) on a ballot (one
vote per Magellan Share) subject to the rights and
restrictions on voting which may attach to or be
imposed on Magellan Shares (at present there are
none);</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The right to receive dividends;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>In a winding up, the right to receive payment in
proportion to the amount paid (if any) to the
holders of Magellan Shares in a liquidating
distribution.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan Shares are 
fully transferable.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The rights attaching
to Magellan Shares may be varied with the approval of Magellan shareholders in
general meeting by special resolution.

<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>7.7 COMPARISON 
OF MPAL AND MAGELLAN SHAREHOLDER RIGHTS</U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">MPAL is incorporated 
under the laws of Australia and Magellan is incorporated under the laws of the
State of Delaware, United States. If MPAL Shareholders participate in the Offer 
and receive
Magellan Shares in exchange for their MPAL Shares, they will become Magellan 
common shareholders.
MPAL&#146;s Shareholders&#146; rights are governed by Australian law and 
regulations, including the
Corporations Act and MPAL&#146;s Constitution. Once the MPAL Shareholders 
accepting the Offer become
Magellan Shareholders, their rights as such will be governed by the Delaware 
General Corporation
Law and by the Magellan Restated Certificate of Incorporation and the Magellan 
By-Laws. The
material differences between the rights of MPAL Shareholders and Magellan 
Shareholders, resulting
from differences in the respective governing documents and the applicable law, 
are set out in
Appendix&nbsp;E.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">MPAL Shareholders 
should have particular regard to the following differences as set out in 
Appendix&nbsp;E:
</DIV>

    <TD width="2%" nowrap align="left">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="2%">&#150;</TD>
    <TD> resolutions to be passed at a Magellan Shareholders meeting must be 
passed by
both a majority of shareholders voting, <I>and </I>by a majority of votes cast 
on the
resolution. This dual approval process is not a feature of Australian law and so
impacts
on the ability of Magellan to receive an affirmative vote on a resolution;</TD>
</TR>

<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U> 7.8  DUAL 
LISTING ISSUES</U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">As Magellan will be 
listed on the ASX as well as maintaining its listings on NASDAQ and the Boston
Stock Exchange, it will be subject to the ASX Listing Rules, NASDAQ Marketplace 
Rules and Boston
Stock Exchange Rules (which are substantially similar to the NASDAQ Marketplace 
Rules).
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The following is a 
brief summary of major rules contained in the ASX Listing Rules and NASDAQ
Marketplace Rules applicable to Magellan.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>(a)&nbsp;ASX 
Listing Rules</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The ASX Listing Rules
sets out the requirements that must be satisfied for an entity to gain
admission to ASX&#146;s Official List and its on-going obligations.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Except for the 
waivers of the Listing Rules granted by ASX identified below, Magellan will be
subject to the Listing Rules as they currently apply to MPAL including the 
following:
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">

transparent">

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Continuous and periodic disclosure obligations in relation to price
sensitive and financial reporting on a quarterly and annual basis
respectively including specific disclosure in relation to mining
entities;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD>Subject to certain exceptions, any issue of securities within a 12
month period beyond 15% of the issued capital of a listed company
requires shareholder approval;</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><I>(ii)&nbsp;The 
13</I><SUP style="font-size: 85%; vertical-align: text-top"><I>th</I></SUP> 
<I>Article</I>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The 13th Article of 
the Magellan Restated Certificate of Incorporation provides that a 
&#147;Business
Combination&#148; with a &#147;Related Person&#148; (including a merger, issue 
of shares worth more than US$5
million or the sale of any assets worth US$5&nbsp;million or more) requires the 
approval of shareholders
holding at least 66<SUP style="font-size: 85%; vertical-align: text-
top">2</SUP>/<SUB>3</SUB>% of the voting power and 66<SUP style="font-size: 85%;
vertical-align: text-top">2</SUP>/<SUB>3</SUB>%
of shareholders present in person or by proxy and who are entitled to vote on 
the resolution.
Magellan is not required to obtain the higher voting requirement in the 13th 
Article for the
purposes of the Offer because it does not constitute a &#147;Business 
Combination&#148; under Article&nbsp;13th
and because of an exception to the higher voting requirement where the 
transaction has been
approved by the Magellan Board.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">In Australia, 
Section&nbsp;602 of the Corporations Act, protects shareholders of a target 
company in a
takeover bid. These principles are not entrenched in U.S. corporate law and, as 
such, the practice
in the U.S. is for certain mechanisms to be built into a company&#146;s 
constituent documents, including
poison pills, pre-emptive rights and &#147;supermajority&#148; voting 
requirements. The 13<SUP style="font-size: 85%; vertical-align: text-
top">th</SUP>
Article of the Magellan Restated Certificate of Incorporation is one mechanism 
used to provide
Magellan shareholders with protection against potentially hostile corporate 
acquirers.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The presence of such 
mechanisms in the constituent documents of a Delaware corporation is customary
in the U.S. and such a provision has been tested and approved in the Delaware 
courts.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>(b)&nbsp;NASDAQ 
Marketplace Rules</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Companies listed on 
NASDAQ are required to meet high standards of corporate governance
outlined in NASDAQ Marketplace Rules. Among the areas NASDAQ corporate 
governance requirements
address are: Distribution of Annual and Interim Reports, Solicitation of 
Proxies, Independent
Directors, Conflicts of Interest, Audit Committees, Shareholder Approval for 
certain specified
transactions, Shareholder Meetings, Stockholder Voting Rights, Quorum 
requirements and the Code of
Conduct requirements.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">NASDAQ-listed 
companies are required to notify NASDAQ when taking certain actions including,
listing a new class of security or additional shares of the sale class, stock 
splits/stock
dividends, cash dividend and distribution notices, change in transfer agent or 
registrar, change in
number of shares outstanding (5% or more), change in company name, trading 
symbol, title of
security or par value.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Companies listed on 
NASDAQ are required to adhere to regulations regarding the disclosure of
material information. &#147;Material information&#148; is information that would
reasonably be expected to
affect the value of a company&#146;s securities or influence investors&#146; 
decisions. NASDAQ requires,
except in unusual circumstances, that NASDAQ-listed companies:
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>disclose, promptly to the public through any Regulation&nbsp;FD-
compliant method (or combination
of methods), material information which would reasonably be expected to affect 
the value of
their securities or influence investors&#146; decisions, and</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>provide NASDAQ MarketWatch advance notice of certain news events to 
permit MarketWatch to
assess the news announcement for materiality and, in certain circumstances, 
implement
temporary trading halts to allow for even dissemination of the material 
news.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">NASDAQ-listed 
companies are required to file with NASDAQ three copies of all reports and other
documents filed or required to be filed with the Securities and Exchange 
Commission. This
requirement is considered fulfiled if the company files the report or document 
with the SEC through
the EDGAR system at www.sec.gov.
</DIV>

Magellan filed its U.S. Registration Statement on Form S-4 containing a joint
prospectus/proxy statement for the Offer with the SEC. The purpose of the U.S. 
Registration
Statement is to:

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(i)</TD>

<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>7.10</U> 
<U>MAGELLAN SHARES OR MAGELLAN CDIS?</U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Accepting MPAL 
Shareholders should carefully consider whether they wish to receive Magellan 
Shares
or Magellan CDIs under the Offer. Whether you choose to receive Magellan Shares 
or Magellan CDIs
will depend, among other things, on your own personal circumstances.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Relevant factors to 
take into account include the following:
