receiver, manager, receiver and manager or controller or execution or
distress or any other process is levied or attempted or imposed
against any of the main undertaking, property or material assets of
that body corporate;</TD>
</TR>
<TR valign="bottom">
    <TD valign="top"><DIV style="margin-left:0px; text-indent:-
0px">&nbsp;</DIV></TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>
<TR valign="bottom">
    <TD valign="top"><DIV style="margin-left:0px; text-indent:-0px">&nbsp;
</DIV></TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">(f)
</TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">that body corporate stops payment or ceases to
carry on the whole
or any material part of its business or threatens to do so;</TD>
</TR>
<TR valign="bottom">
    <TD valign="top"><DIV style="margin-left:0px; text-indent:-
0px">&nbsp;</DIV></TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>
<TR valign="bottom">
    <TD valign="top"><DIV style="margin-left:0px; text-indent:-0px">&nbsp;
</DIV></TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">(g)
</TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">an order for payment is made or judgement is 
entered or signed
against that body corporate in an amount of not less than A$100,000
and is not satisfied, stayed or set aside within 5 Business Days;</TD>
</TR>
<TR valign="bottom">
    <TD valign="top"><DIV style="margin-left:0px; text-indent:-
0px">&nbsp;</DIV></TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>
<TR valign="bottom">
    <TD valign="top"><DIV style="margin-left:0px; text-indent:-0px">&nbsp;
</DIV></TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">(h)
</TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">that body corporate becomes insolvent or 
unable to pay its debts;</TD>
</TR>
<!-- End Table Body -->
</TABLE>

<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>12.2</U> 
<U>INTERPRETATION </U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">In this Bidder&#146;s
Statement, unless the context requires otherwise:
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>a reference to a word includes the singular and the plural of the word 
and vice versa;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>a reference to a person in this Bidder&#146;s Statement or any other 
document or agreement
includes its successors and permitted assigns;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>a reference to a gender includes any gender;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">(d)</TD>
<TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>a reference to an item in a Section, Schedule, Annexure or Appendix is a
reference to an item
in the section of or schedule, annexure or appendix to this Bidder&#146;s 
Statement and references
to this Bidder&#146;s Statement include its schedules and any annexures;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">(e)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>if a word or phrase is defined, then other parts of speech and 
grammatical forms of that word
or phrase have a corresponding meaning;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">(f)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>a term which refers to a natural person includes a company, a 
partnership, an association, a
corporation, a body corporate, a joint venture or a governmental agency;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">(g)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>headings are included for convenience only and do not affect 
interpretation;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>

transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">(h)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>a reference to a document or agreement including this Bidder&#146;s 
Statement, includes a
reference to that document or agreement as amended, novated, supplemented, 
varied or replaced
from time to time;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">(i)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>a reference to a thing includes a part of that thing and includes but is
not limited to a
right;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background:

not exclude a reference to other items of the same class or genus;</TD>

<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 12pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>13. APPROVAL OF 
BIDDER&#146;S STATEMENT</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><U>1. OFFER</U>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">1.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Magellan offers to acquire your MPAL Shares on the terms and conditions 
of this Offer. You
may accept this Offer in respect of all of your MPAL Shares.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">

    <TD>The consideration being offered by Magellan is 7 fully paid Magellan 
Shares issued for every
10 MPAL Shares.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If you have a registered address in the MPAL Register:</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="2%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>in the United States, you will receive your share consideration in the 
form of
Magellan Shares (traded primarily on NASDAQ);</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="2%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>in Australia you will be offered your share consideration in the form of
either</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:

transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(i)</TD>
<TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Magellan Shares; or</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background:

    <TD>Magellan CDIs (to be traded in the ASX). One Magellan CDI will be issued

accepting this Offer. If you do not choose the form of Offer Consideration on 
your
Acceptance Form, you are deemed to have chosen to receive your Offer 
Consideration
in the form of Magellan CDIs; and</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>

receive

be undertaking the actions set out in Clause 1.7.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt; margin-left: 
2%">Whatever form of share consideration you receive, it will be equivalent to 7
Magellan Shares
for every 10 MPAL Shares.
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If you accept this Offer and Magellan acquires your MPAL Shares, 
Magellan is also entitled to
any Rights in respect of those MPAL Shares.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">

10pt">

transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">1.5</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The number of MPAL Shares that you hold may mean that, if you accept 
this Offer, you will be
entitled to a number of Magellan Shares or Magellan Shares in the form of 
Magellan CDIs that
is not a whole number. In this case, your entitlement to Magellan Shares or

the form of Magellan CDIs will be rounded up to the next greater whole 
number.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Magellan intends for any Magellan Shares in the form of Magellan CDIs 
issued pursuant to the
Offer to be listed on ASX after the Offer has been completed. This Offer is 
subject to a
condition that the application for admission to quotation of Magellan Shares in 
the form of
Magellan CDIs issued pursuant to this Offer is made within seven days from the 
commencement of
the Offer Period and permission for admission to quotation is granted no later 
than seven days
after the end of the Offer Period.</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">1.7</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If you are a Foreign Shareholder and you accept the Offer, Magellan 
will:</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">

    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(a)</TD>
<TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>arrange for the allotment to a nominee approved by ASIC (<B>Nominee</B>)
of the number
of Magellan Shares in the form of Magellan CDIs to be issued in accordance with 
the
Offer to which you and all other Foreign Shareholders will have been entitled 
but for
this Clause 1.7;</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background:

    <TD width="2%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>cause those Magellan Shares in the form of Magellan CDIs so allotted to 
be
offered for sale within 21&nbsp;days of the end of the Offer Period in such a

price and on such other terms and conditions as are determined by the

</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background:

    <TD width="2%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>cause the Nominee to pay to you the amount (<B>Offer Payment Amount</B>)
ascertained in
accordance with the following formula:</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt; margin-left: 2%">Net 
Proceeds of Sale X NCS/TCS
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt; margin-left: 2%">= 
Offer Payment Amount
</DIV>
<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">-80-
</DIV>
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt; margin-left: 
2%">Where:
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt; margin-left: 
2%"><B>Net Proceeds of Sale </B>means the amount (if any) remaining after 
deducting from the proceeds of
the sale of the Magellan Shares in the form of Magellan CDIs to which the 
Foreign
Shareholders would be entitled under this Offer but for this Clause 1.7 the 
expenses of the
sale of the Magellan Shares in the form of Magellan CDIs allotted to the Nominee
under this
Clause 1.7.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt; margin-left: 
2%"><B>NCS </B>means the number of Magellan Shares in the form of Magellan CDIs 
to which you would be
entitled under this Offer but for this Clause 1.7.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt; margin-left: 
2%"><B>TCS </B>means total number of Magellan Shares in the form of Magellan 
CDIs allotted to the
Nominee under this Clause 1.7 in respect of Magellan Shares in the form of 
Magellan CDIs held
by Foreign Shareholders.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt; margin-left: 
2%">Payment of the Offer Payment Amount will be made by cheque in Australian 
dollars. The cheque
will be sent to you at your risk by pre-paid airmail to your address as shown on
the MPAL
Register as at the date the Offer Payment Amount is calculated. Under no 
circumstances will
interest be paid to accepting MPAL Shareholders on the proceeds of this sale, 
regardless of
any reasonable delay in remitting these proceeds to you.
</DIV>

PERIOD</U>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt; margin-left: 
2%">Unless withdrawn, this Offer remains open for acceptance during the period 
commencing on the
date of this Offer and ending at 7.00pm on &#091;&nbsp; &#093; Sydney time, 
subject to any extension of
that period in accordance with sections 650C and 650D of the Corporations Act.

<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 12pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>APPENDIX B: ASX 
ANNOUNCEMENT REGARDING OFFER</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><IMG 
src="y13986a1y1398608.gif" alt="(MPC LOGO)">
</DIV>
<DIV align="center" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 18pt"><B>MAGELLAN 
PETROLEUM CORPORATION ANNOUNCES OFFER<BR>
FOR MINORITY INTEREST IN MAGELLAN PETROLEUM AUSTRALIA LIMITED</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">HARTFORD, Conn., 
United States, SYDNEY, Australia October&nbsp;18, 2005 &#150; Magellan Petroleum
Corporation (NASDAQ Capital Market &#151; trading symbol MPET) 
(&#147;Magellan&#148;) today announced its
intention to commence an exchange offer (the &#147;Offer&#148;) to acquire all 
of the ordinary shares of
Magellan Petroleum Australia Limited (&#147;MPAL&#148;) (Australian Stock 
Exchange &#150; code MAG) that it does
not currently own. Magellan currently has a 55.13% ownership interest in MPAL.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The Offer 
consideration will be seven (7)&nbsp;newly-issued shares of Magellan common 
stock for each ten
(10)&nbsp;outstanding MPAL shares. If the Offer is successful, new Magellan 
shares will be issued to
MPAL&#146;s Australian shareholders in the form of CDIs (CHESS Depository 
Interests), which will be
listed on the Australian Stock Exchange (&#147;ASX&#148;).
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Based on 
Magellan&#146;s closing share price of US$1.93 on October&nbsp;17, 2005 on the 
NASDAQ Capital Market
and an A$/US$ exchange rate of 0.75, the Offer values MPAL at 
A$84.1&nbsp;million in total (including
the shares currently owned by Magellan), or A$1.80 per share. Accordingly, the 
proposed
consideration in aggregate for the 44.87% of MPAL&#146;s shares which Magellan
does not already own is
approximately 14.7&nbsp;million Magellan shares, with an aggregate value of 
A$37.7&nbsp;million based on the
above.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan has retained
TM Capital Corp. of New York, N.Y. and Baron Partners Limited of Sydney,
Australia to serve as its financial advisers in relation to the Offer.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The Offer 
consideration exceeds the highest price at which MPAL shares have traded since 
January
2003 and represents a premium of:
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>approximately 28% to MPAL&#146;s volume weighted average price of A$1.41
in the 3-month period prior to this announcement; and</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>approximately 33% to MPAL&#146;s closing share price of A$1.35 on 
October&nbsp;18, 2005.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Following successful 
completion of the Offer and the compulsory acquisition, non-Magellan
shareholders of MPAL would collectively own approximately 36.3% of 
Magellan&#146;s issued and
outstanding shares.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>Offer Timing 
&#038; Conditions</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan intends, as 
soon as practicable, to file with the U.S. Securities and Exchange
Commission a Registration Statement on Form S-4, which will contain a 
prospectus/proxy statement in
connection with the proposed Offer.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">A Bidder&#146;s 
Statement will be filed with ASX and the Australian Securities and Investments
Commission as soon as practicable. A copy of the Bidder&#146;s Statement will 
also be posted to MPAL
shareholders and made available on Magellan&#146;s website at: www.magpet.com.
</DIV>
<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">-89-
</DIV>
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan anticipates 
that the Offer will remain open for a minimum of eight (8)&nbsp;weeks after the
dispatch of the Bidder&#146;s Statement to MPAL&#146;s shareholders.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The Offer will be 
subject to certain conditions including Magellan acquiring at least 90% of 
MPAL&#146;s
outstanding shares on or before the end of the prescribed Offer Period, and 
approval of the
issuance of Magellan common stock in the Offer by Magellan&#146;s shareholders 
at the upcoming 2005
annual meeting of shareholders. Other conditions to the Offer are more fully 
described in the
attached Schedule&nbsp;A.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>Benefits
to MPAL Shareholders</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan believes 
that the benefits of the Offer for MPAL and its shareholders are numerous.
While retaining an interest in the underlying MPAL assets and business 
prospects, MPAL shareholders
will enjoy the following benefits:
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>a value premium of 28% on MPAL&#146;s volume weighted average trading 
price on the ASX for the last 3&nbsp;months;</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>shares in a more liquid security with significantly higher average 
trading volumes;</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>potentially cheaper access to capital;</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>potential cost savings from organisational efficiencies arising from the
simplified capital structure;</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>tax roll-over relief under Australian law; and</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>full alignment of the strategies of both companies.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan&#146;s 
Chairman, Mr.&nbsp;Walter McCann, said: &#147;We believe that the current 
shareholding structure
of MPAL is not necessarily in the best interests of either Magellan or MPAL 
shareholders. We also
believe that the existing ownership structure has not provided optimal benefits 
in transparency as
to pricing or market understanding of MPAL&#146;s assets nor fostered liquidity 
or access to capital in
either the United States or Australia. We believe that a successful takeover 
will lead to a
stronger company which will be better positioned to thrive in the current 
competitive atmosphere
and to improve overall shareholder returns.&#148;
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>Magellan&#146;s 
Intentions if the Offer is Successful</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">It is Magellan&#146;s
present intention, following the completion of the Offer, to maintain the
current board of directors of MPAL and to own 100% of MPAL&#146;s outstanding 
shares.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan&#146;s 
specific intentions for the near term future of MPAL will be described in 
Magellan&#146;s
relevant U.S. and Australian regulatory filings. In summary, Magellan envisages 
the following with
respect to the continuation of the business, the position of the employees and 
the protection of
MPAL&#146;s assets:
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Business</B>: Magellan expects MPAL to continue as an oil and gas
exploration and production company in substantially the same manner as
it is presently operated.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background:
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Board of Directors and Executive Management</B>: Magellan will 
maintain
the current board of directors. Magellan will also seek to retain key
members of the MPAL executive management team, whose performance will
continue to be reviewed in line with current procedures. Additional
members of the executive management team will be added, as
appropriate.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Employees and Consultants</B>: Magellan intends to continue the 
monitoring
and review process which is currently in place in regard to MPAL&#146;s
employees and the usage of consultancy services.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>Headquarters</B>: MPAL, as a wholly-owned subsidiary of Magellan, 
will
continue to be headquartered in Brisbane. Magellan&#146;s headquarters will
continue to be based in Hartford, Connecticut, USA.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>MPAL Business Policies and Practices</B>: Consistent with 
Magellan&#146;s
enhanced ownership position, Magellan intends to continue to review
MPAL&#146;s important business policies and practices, including corporate
governance, exploration and development efforts, capital expenditures,
existing and planned joint ventures, acquisition prospects, and
investment policies, with the aim to maximise overall shareholder
return.</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>

<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>About Magellan</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Magellan was 
established in 1957, and was incorporated in the State of Delaware in 1967.
Magellan&#146;s common stock is quoted on the NASDAQ Capital Market (symbol: 
MPET). The company is
engaged in the sale of oil and gas resulting from the exploration for and 
development of oil and
gas reserves. Magellan&#146;s most significant asset is its 55.13% equity 
ownership interest in MPAL.
Magellan also has a direct 2.67% carried interest in the Kotaneelee Gas Field in
the Yukon
Territory of Canada. Magellan has approximately 6,750 record shareholders.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>About MPAL</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">MPAL was established 
in 1964, and is headquartered in Brisbane, Australia. MPAL shares are
quoted on the ASX. The company is engaged in the sale of oil and gas resulting 
from the exploration
for and development of oil and gas reserves. The company&#146;s oil and gas 
production assets are
principally located in the Amadeus Basin of the Northern Territory in Australia,
where MPAL
operates the Palm Valley gas field. Other reserves and prospects are located 
elsewhere in
Australia, and also in New Zealand and the United Kingdom. MPAL has 
approximately 1,790 record
shareholders.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt"><B>Forward Looking 
Statements</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">Statements in this 
release which are not historical in nature are intended to be, and are
hereby identified as, forward-looking statements for purposes of the Private 
Securities Litigation
Reform Act of 1995. These statements about Magellan and MPAL relate to their 
businesses and
prospects, revenues, expenses, operating cash flows, the benefits of the 
proposed Offer, and other
matters that involve a number of uncertainties that may cause actual results to 
differ materially
from expectations. Among these risks and uncertainties are the successful 
completion of the Offer,
pricing and production levels from the properties in which Magellan and MPAL 
have interests, the
extent of the recoverable reserves at those properties, the future outcome of 
the negotiations for
gas sales contracts for the remaining uncontracted reserves at both the Mereenie
and Palm Valley
gas fields in the Amadeus Basin. In addition, MPAL has a large number of 
exploration permits and
faces the risk that any wells drilled may fail to encounter hydrocarbons in 
commercially
recoverable quantities. Any forward-looking information provided in this release
should be
considered with these factors in mind. Magellan assumes no obligation to update 
any forward-looking
statements contained in this release, whether as a result of new information, 
future events or
otherwise.

threatened against MPAL or a controlled entity of MPAL which are material in the
context of
MPAL&#146;s operations as a whole;</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:
10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">11.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>No regulatory intervention</B>: During the period commencing on the 
Announcement Date and ending
on the expiry of the Offer Period, no governmental agency or any other person 
takes any action
to:</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:

    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD>prohibit, prevent or inhibit the acquisition of, or trading in, MPAL 
shares;</TD>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="2%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>impose conditions on the Offer which impose unduly onerous obligations 
upon
Magellan or would materially affect the business or capital structure of MPAL; 
or</TD>
</TR>
<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: 
transparent">
    <TD width="2%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>require the divestiture by Magellan of securities or assets of any MPAL 
group
Entity;</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt; margin-left: 
2%">other than an application to or a decision or order of ASIC or the Takeovers
Panel for the
purpose of or in the exercise of the powers and discretions conferred on it by 
the
Corporations Act;
</DIV>
<DIV style="margin-top: 6pt">
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size:

transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">12.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>

separate
condition):</TD>

    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the shares of MPAL or any of the controlled entities of MPAL are 
converted into a
larger or smaller number of shares;</TD>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>MPAL or a controlled entity of MPAL resolves to reduce its share capital
in any
way;</TD>

<TR>
    <TD style="font-size: 6pt">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR><TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background:

    <TD width="2%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="3%" nowrap align="left">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>MPAL or a controlled entity of MPAL:</TD>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>No selective disclosure of information</B>: At all times during the

provides to Magellan a copy of all information that is not generally available 
(within the

MPAL or any of
their respective businesses or operations that has been provided by MPAL or any 
of their
respective officers, employees, advisers or agents to any person (other than 
Magellan) for the
purposes of soliciting, encouraging or facilitating a proposal or offer by that 
person, or by
any other person, in relation to a transaction under which:</TD>

<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 12pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>APPENDIX E: 
COMPARISON OF MPAL AND MAGELLAN SHAREHOLDER RIGHTS</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The following summary
does not contain all the information that may be important to MPAL
Shareholders and is qualified in its entirety by reference to the laws of 
Delaware and Australia
and the governing corporate documents of Magellan and MPAL. Magellan will 
provide a copy of each of
the Magellan Restated Certificate of Incorporation, the Magellan By Laws and 
MPAL Constitution free
of charge on request. To obtain a copy, please contact Magellan&#146;s 
information agent in Australia,
Georgeson Shareholder (contact details shown in Corporate Directory).
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 12pt"><B>Authorised 
Capital Stock</B>
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">As at the date of 
this Bidder&#146;s Statement, there were 46,691,944 MPAL Shares on issue.
</DIV>
<DIV align="left" style="font-size: 10pt; margin-top: 6pt">The Magellan Restated
Certificate of Incorporation currently authorises 200,000,000 shares of
common stock, par value $0.01 per share. As at the date of this Bidder&#146;s 
Statement, there were
25,783,243 Magellan Shares on issue.
</DIV>
<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">-97-
</DIV>

<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">
<DIV align="center">
<TABLE style="font-size: 10pt" cellspacing="0" border="0" cellpadding="0" 
width="100%">
<!-- Begin Table Head -->
<TR valign="bottom">
    <TD width="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="2%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="40%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TR style="font-size: 8pt" valign="bottom">
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD nowrap align="center" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #000000"><B>Rights
of holders of MPAL Shares</B></TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD nowrap align="center" style="border-bottom: 1px solid #000000"><B>Rights
of holders of Magellan Shares</B></TD>
</TR>
<!-- End Table Head -->
<!-- Begin Table Body -->
<TR valign="bottom">
    <TD valign="top"><DIV style="margin-left:0px; text-indent:-
0px"><B>Shareholder Voting<BR>
Rights</B>
</DIV></TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">Each MPAL Share (subject to any specific terms
of issue) confers a right to vote at all
general meetings. On a show of hands, each
MPAL Shareholder present in person, or by
proxy, representative or attorney, has 1 vote.
If a poll is held, MPAL Shareholders present
in person or by their proxy, representative or
attorney will have 1 vote for each fully paid
MPAL Share held (and the equivalent fraction
for partly paid shares).<BR><BR>
The constitution provides that a poll may be
demanded by the chairman of the general
meeting, at least 5 voting members, or by
members holding either not less than 10% of
the total voting rights of all members having
the right to vote at the meeting or holding
shares conferring a right to vote at the
meeting on which an aggregate sum has been
paid equal to not less than 10% of the total
sum paid on all MPAL Shares conferring that
right. However, the Corporations Act also
allows shareholders with at least 5% of the
votes that may be cast on the resolution on a
poll to demand a poll.<BR><BR>
Unless the Corporations Act or the
constitution requires a special resolution,
resolutions are passed by a simple majority of
votes cast on the resolution.<BR><BR>
Under the Corporations Act, a special
resolution may be passed by the company if not
less than 28&nbsp;days&#146; notice of a general meeting
is given, specifying the intention to propose
the special resolution and stating the
resolution. A special resolution must be
passed by at least 75% of the votes cast by
shareholders entitled to vote.
</TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">All voting rights are vested in the holders of
Common Stock, each share voting equally with
every other share. A 1968 Amendment to the
Magellan Restated Certificate of Incorporation
by the addition of the 12<SUP style="font-size: 85%; vertical-align: text-
top">th</SUP> Article,
provides that in matters to be voted on at
meetings of shareholders, the vote of a
majority of those present in person or by proxy
will be required in addition to a majority of
the shares represented. The 12<SUP style="font-size: 85%; vertical-align: text-
top">th</SUP>
Article provides that when shares are held by
members or shareholders of another company,
association or similar entity and such persons
act in concert, or when shares are held by or
for a group of shareholders whose members act
in concert by virtue of any contract, agreement
or understanding, such persons shall be deemed
to be 1 shareholder for the purposes of the
12<SUP style="font-size: 85%; vertical-align: text-top">th</SUP> Article. 
Magellan has the power
to determine whether shareholders are acting in
concert, depending on the circumstances and the
evidence, if any, that shareholders were in
fact so acting and should therefore be treated
as 1 shareholder.<BR><BR>
Section&nbsp;6 of Article&nbsp;II of the Magellan By-Laws
provides that at all meetings of the
shareholders, subject to the provisions of the
Magellan Restated Certificate of Incorporation
and Section&nbsp;8 of Article&nbsp;II of the Magellan
By-Laws, each shareholder having the right to
vote at such meeting is entitled to one vote
for each share standing registered in his name
on the date for such a meeting.</TD>

</DIV></TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">The Corporations Act requires certain matters
to be resolved by a company by special
resolution, including:<BR><BR>
<DIV style="margin-left:10px; text-indent:-10px"><B>&#149;</B> the change of 
name of the company;</DIV><BR>
<DIV style="margin-left:10px; text-indent:-10px"><B>&#149;</B> a selective 
reduction of capital or selective buy-back;</DIV><BR>
<DIV style="margin-left:10px; text-indent:-10px"><B>&#149;</B> the conversion of
the company from one type or form to another; and</DIV><BR>
<DIV style="margin-left:10px; text-indent:-10px"><B>&#149;</B> a decision to 
wind-up the company voluntarily.</DIV><BR>
The Corporations Act requires voting by
separate classes of MPAL Shares only with
respect to a variation of class rights.
</TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">Section&nbsp;8 of Article&nbsp;II provides 
that all
elections will be by ballot and any matter to
be voted on at the shareholders&#146; meeting must
be approved, not only by a majority of the
shares voted at such meeting (or such greater
number of shares as would otherwise be required
by law or the Magellan Restated Certificate of
Incorporation), but also by a majority of the
shareholders present in person or by proxy. In
the case of the election of Directors, if no
candidate receives both such majorities then
each person who receives the majority in number
of the shareholders present in person or by
proxy will be entitled to fill such vacancies
by virtue of having received such majority.<BR><BR>
When shares are held by members or shareholders
of another company, association or similar
entity and such persons act in concert, or when
the shares are held by a group of shareholders
whose members act in concert by virtue of any
contract, agreement or understanding, such
persons will be deemed to be one shareholder
for the purposes of Section&nbsp;8 of Article&nbsp;II.</TD>

    <TD valign="top"><DIV style="margin-left:0px; text-indent:-
0px"><B>Restrictions on
issues of
securities</B>
</DIV></TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">Under the MPAL Constitution, the MPAL
directors may allot or otherwise dispose of
shares with preferred, deferred or other
rights subject to such restrictions as to
dividends, voting, return of capital, payment
of calls or otherwise to such persons and on
such terms and conditions as they think fit.
<BR><BR>ASX Listing Rule&nbsp;7.1 requires MPAL Shareholder
approval if MPAL wishes to issue 15% or more
of its capital in any 12&nbsp;month period, unless
an exception applies. Exceptions include
issues under offers to all ordinary
shareholders in proportion to their respective
holdings, issues under takeover bids or
schemes of arrangements and issues under
dividend reinvestment plans.
<BR><BR>The MPAL Constitution provides that the MPAL
directors must not, without the prior approval
of MPAL Shareholders, issue shares or grant
options which would (on exercise of the
option) result in the transfer of a
controlling interest in MPAL, or result in 50%
or more of the votes exercisable on a poll,
being registered in the name of the transferee
except if an offer of shares or options has
been made to all ordinary shareholders in
proportion to their respective shareholding.
<BR><BR>Under the MPAL Constitution, an MPAL director
and his or her Associates cannot participate
in the issue of MPAL Shares or grant options
unless MPAL has first by special resolution
approved the number of shares or options to be
issued to the director or associate or except
in cases permitted by the ASX Listing Rules.
This does not apply to pro rata issues or
issues to executive directors.
<BR><BR>ASX Listing Rules&nbsp;10.11 and 10.14 allow the
issue of shares or options to directors with
the approval of shareholders by ordinary
resolution.
</TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">Under the Magellan Restated Certificate of
Incorporation, the Directors have the power to
issue additional Magellan Shares.<BR><BR>
Nasdaq Marketplace Rules require shareholder
approval prior to the issuance of additional
Magellan Shares in the following circumstances:<BR><BR>
<DIV style="margin-left:20px; text-indent:-20px">(a)&nbsp;when the issue or 
potential issue will
result in a change of control of Magellan;</DIV><BR>
<DIV style="margin-left:20px; text-indent:-20px">(b)&nbsp;in connection with the
acquisition of the
stock or assets of another company if:</DIV><BR>
<DIV style="margin-left:40px; text-indent:-15px">(i)&nbsp;any director, officer 
or substantial
shareholder of Magellan has a 5% or greater
interest (or such persons collectively have a
10% or greater interest), directly or
indirectly, in the company or assets to be
acquired or in the consideration to be paid in
the transaction or series of related
transactions and the present or potential
issuance of common stock, or securities
convertible into or exercisable for common
stock, could result in an increase in
outstanding common shares or voting power of 5%
or more; or</DIV><BR>
<DIV style="margin-left:40px; text-indent:-15px">(ii)&nbsp;where, due to the 
present or potential
issue of Magellan Shares, or securities
convertible into or exercisable for Magellan
Shares, other than a public offering for cash:</DIV><BR>
<DIV style="margin-left:60px; text-indent:-25px">(A)&nbsp;the Magellan Shares 
have or will have upon
issuance voting power equal to or in excess of
20% of the voting power outstanding before the
issuance of stock or securities convertible
into or exercisable for Magellan Shares; or</DIV><BR>
<DIV style="margin-left:60px; text-indent:-25px">(B)&nbsp;the number of Magellan
Shares to be issued
is or will be equal to or in excess of 20% of
the number of Magellan Shares outstanding
before the issuance of the stock or securities;
or</DIV><BR>
<DIV style="margin-left:20px; text-indent:-20px">(c)&nbsp;in connection with a 
transaction other than
a public offering involving:<BR><BR></DIV>
<DIV style="margin-left:20px; text-indent:-20px">(i)&nbsp;the sale, issue or 
potential issue by
Magellan of Magellan Shares (or securities
convertible into or exercisable for Magellan
Shares) at a price less than the greater of
book or market value which together with sales
by officers, directors or substantial
shareholders of Magellan equals 20% or more of
Magellan Shares or 20% or more of the voting
power outstanding before the issuance; or</DIV><BR>
<DIV style="margin-left:20px; text-indent:-20px">(ii)&nbsp;the sale, issuance or
potential issuance
by Magellan
of Magellan Shares (or securities
convertible into or exercisable Magellan
Shares) equal to 20% or more of the Magellan
Shares or 20% or more of the voting power
outstanding before the issuance for less than
the greater of book or market value of the
shares.</DIV></TD>

<!-- End Table Head -->
<!-- Begin Table Body -->
<TR valign="bottom">
    <TD valign="top"><DIV style="margin-left:0px; text-indent:-
0px"><B>Amending<BR>
constituent<BR>
documents</B>
</DIV></TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">Under the Corporations Act, a company may by
special resolution (75% of shareholders who
vote) amend or repeal its constitution or any
provision of its constitution. The
Corporations Act requires voting by separate
classes of shares only if the amendment to the
constitution varies class rights.
</TD>
    <TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD align="left" valign="top">Under the Delaware General Corporation Law and
the Magellan Restated Certificate of
Incorporation, a proposed amendment to the
Restated Certificate of Incorporation,
including but not limited to an amendment to
change the number or type of shares of
authorised capital stock, requires:<BR><BR>
<DIV style="margin-left:10px; text-indent:-10px"><B>&#149;</B> the approval of 
the board of directors;</DIV><BR>
<DIV style="margin-left:10px; text-indent:-10px"><B>&#149;</B> the affirmative 
vote of a majority of the
outstanding shares entitled to vote on the
matter; and</DIV><BR>
<DIV style="margin-left:10px; text-indent:-10px"><B>&#149;</B> the affirmative 
vote of a majority of the
outstanding shares of each class entitled to
vote thereon as a class.</DIV><BR>
If an amendment would change the aggregate
number of authorised shares of a particular
class or series of shares, change the par value
of the shares of such class or series or alter
the powers, preferences or special rights of
the shares of such class or series so as to
affect them adversely, a majority of the
outstanding shares of that class or series,
voting as a class, also must vote to authorise
the amendment.<BR><BR>
Article&nbsp;12<SUP style="font-size: 85%; vertical-align: text-top">th</SUP> of
the Magellan
Restated Certificate of Incorporation provides
that in matters to be voted on at meetings of
shareholders, the vote of a majority of those
present in person or by proxy will be required
in addition to a majority of the shares
represented. Article&nbsp;12<SUP style="font-size: 85%; vertical-align: text-
top">th</SUP> provides
that when shares are held by members or
shareholders of another company, association or
similar entity and such persons act in concert,
or when shares are held by or for a group of
shareholders whose members act in concert by
virtue of any contract, agreement or
understanding, such persons shall be deemed to
be one shareholder for the purposes of Article
12<SUP style="font-size: 85%; vertical-align: text-top">th</SUP>.<BR><BR>
Under the Delaware General Corporation Law, a
proposed amendment to a Delaware corporation&#146;s
Certificate of Incorporation requires an
affirmative vote of a majority of all shares
entitled to vote thereon. If any such amendment
would adversely affect the rights of any
shareholders of a particular class or series of
shares, the vote of the majority of all
outstanding shares of that class or series,
voting as a class is also necessary to
authorise the amendment.<BR><BR>
Under the Delaware General Corporation Law, the
power to adopt, alter and repeal a Delaware
corporation&#146;s By-Laws is vested in the
shareholders, except to the extent that the
Certificate of Incorporation also vests such
powers in the Board of Directors. The Magellan
Restated Certificate of Incorporation grants
these powers to the Board of Directors. This
grant of authority does not limit the power of
the shareholders to adopt, amend or repeal the
Magellan By-Laws.<BR><BR>
The Magellan By-Laws may be altered, amended or
repealed by a vote of a majority of the
directors at any regular or special meeting of
the Board or by the shareholders at a meeting
called for that purpose by the favourable vote
of 66<SUP style="font-size: 85%; vertical-align: text-top">2</SUP>/<SUB>3</SUB>%
of the voting
power of all outstanding voting shares
generally entitled to vote at such meeting and
66<SUP style="font-size: 85%; vertical-align: text-top">2</SUP>/<SUB>3</SUB>% of
the
shareholders present in person or by proxy and
entitled to vote at such meeting.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>
<DIV style="font-family: Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif">
<DIV align="center">
<TABLE style="font-size: 10pt" cellspacing="0" border="0" cellpadding="0"

<!-- Begin Table Head -->

    <TD width="20%">&nbsp;</TD>
